  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>Additions</h2>
<ul>
<li>Indicate which commits have not yet been pushed to the remote in "History" tab - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="369076150" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/5873" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/5873/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/5873">desktop#5873</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Fixes and improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Use upstream repository in commit message links to GitHub - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="586050868" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9334" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9334/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9334">desktop#9334</a></li>
<li>Reset scroll position to the top of the history tab after switching repositories - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="586205792" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9341" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9341/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9341">desktop#9341</a></li>
<li>Allow user to cancel rebase flow when warned about force pushing - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="598434563" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9507" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9507/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9507">desktop#9507</a></li>
<li>Update embedded Git to address security vulnerability</li>
<li>Display pull requests from upstream repository in pull request list - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="389508250" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/6383" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/6383/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/6383">desktop#6383</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Linux-specific packaging fixes</h2>
<ul>
<li>Improve handling of symlink cleanup when uninstalling <code>deb</code> package - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="599449425" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/253" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/pull/253/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/pull/253">#253</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jfgordon2/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jfgordon2">@jfgordon2</a>!</li>
<li>Set <code>setuid</code> bit for <code>chrome-sandbox</code> executable for <code>deb</code> package - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="599833709" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/254" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/pull/254/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/pull/254">#254</a></li>
</ul>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <p>This release contains numerous Linux-specific improvements, and I want to give a huge shout out to <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jfgordon2/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jfgordon2">@jfgordon2</a> who helped with all of these.</p>
<h2>New Features</h2>
<ul>
<li>CLI support for launching GitHub Desktop - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="583989943" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/231" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/pull/231/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/pull/231">#231</a> <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="589905202" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/239" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/pull/239/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/pull/239">#239</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jfgordon2/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jfgordon2">@jfgordon2</a>!</li>
</ul>
<p>After installing the <code>deb</code> package, a symlink is added at <code>/usr/bin/github</code>, enabling the user to run <code>github</code> from the terminal to launch (or focus if already open) GitHub Desktop.</p>
<ul>
<li>Added editor and shell integration for Elementary OS - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="583989943" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/231" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/pull/231/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/pull/231">#231</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jfgordon2/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jfgordon2">@jfgordon2</a>!</li>
</ul>
<h2>Fixes and improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Scrollbar remains white in dark mode - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="589447115" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/236" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/issues/236/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/236">#236</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jfgordon2/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jfgordon2">@jfgordon2</a>!</li>
<li>About dialog now links to releases in this repository - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="590048505" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/issues/241" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/shiftkey/desktop/pull/241/hovercard" href="https://github.com/shiftkey/desktop/pull/241">#241</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/jfgordon2/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/jfgordon2">@jfgordon2</a>!</li>
</ul>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>New Features</h2>
<ul>
<li>Set Git proxy environment variables from system configuration automatically - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="569101754" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9154" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/9154/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/9154">desktop#9154</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Additions</h2>
<ul>
<li>Enable creating a GitHub issue from app menu and keyboard shortcut <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="555660145" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8989" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8989/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8989">desktop#8989</a></li>
<li>Support keyboard scrolling in diffs <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="562146096" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9074" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9074/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9074">desktop#9074</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Fixes and improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Ensure branch protection warning works when branch names contain special characters <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="562699049" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9086" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/9086/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/9086">desktop#9086</a></li>
<li>Ensure intro page is responsive when resizing the window <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="570715682" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9175" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9175/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9175">desktop#9175</a></li>
<li>Ensure local branch is also deleted when deleting a branch that no longer exists on the remote <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="541505738" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8831" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8831/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8831">desktop#8831</a></li>
<li>Restore negative space in "Files selected" graphic for Dark Theme <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="529625918" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8716" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8716/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8716">desktop#8716</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/say25/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/say25">@say25</a>!</li>
<li>Support selecting text in error dialogs <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="447265090" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7606" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7606/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7606">desktop#7606</a></li>
<li>Prevent bringing changes to another branch from failing silently <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="559251296" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9038" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/9038/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/9038">desktop#9038</a></li>
<li>Save the user's position within "History" and "Changes" tabs when switching <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="561025750" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9061" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9061/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9061">desktop#9061</a></li>
<li>Update the remote url when a repository's name changes on GitHub <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="518095010" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8590" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8590/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8590">desktop#8590</a></li>
<li>Allow "Open in Desktop" button from pull requests on GitHub to open in a local fork in Desktop <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="557659011" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9012" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9012/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9012">desktop#9012</a></li>
<li>Format errors containing raw Git output with fixed-width font <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="554221786" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8964" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/8964/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/8964">desktop#8964</a></li>
<li>Modify "View on GitHub" menu item to open upstream for local fork repositories <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="583941947" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9316" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/9316/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/9316">desktop#9316</a></li>
<li>Create new branches in forks from the default branch of the upstream repo <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="454553205" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7762" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7762/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7762">desktop#7762</a></li>
<li>Graduate Dark Theme out of beta <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="582274485" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9294" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/9294/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/9294">desktop#9294</a>"</li>
</ul>
<p>For more information check out the <a href="https://desktop.github.com/release-notes/">release notes</a> on <a href="https://desktop.github.com/release-notes/">desktop.github.com</a>.</p>

  <div class="markdown-body">
    <h2>New Features</h2>
<ul>
<li>Prompt users to create a fork if they fail to push to a GitHub repository due to permissions - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="514060986" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8548" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8548/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8548">desktop#8548</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Additions</h2>
<ul>
<li>Show link to upstream pull requests in pull request list of a fork - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="554265229" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8965" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/8965/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/8965">desktop#8965</a></li>
<li>Show a warning if the user doesn't have write access to push to the repository and offer to make a fork - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="551556412" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8938" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8938/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8938">desktop#8938</a></li>
<li>Provide configuration in Preferences to always bring or leave changes when switching branches - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="454171946" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7746" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7746/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7746">desktop#7746</a></li>
<li>Prompt users to re-authorize if required by any of their GitHub organizations - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="549098241" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8910" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/8910/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/8910">desktop#8910</a></li>
</ul>
<h2>Fixes and improvements</h2>
<ul>
<li>Don't display erroneous Git error when creating a fork - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="557021612" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9004" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/9004/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9004">desktop#9004</a></li>
<li>Remove stray characters from Git progress indicators on Windows - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="557013920" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/9003" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/9003/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/9003">desktop#9003</a>"</li>
<li>Show proper dialog when push fails due to missing workflow scope - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="553753595" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8958" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/8958/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/8958">desktop#8958</a></li>
<li>Take users to the correct page on GitHub.com when opening a pull request in browser from a fork - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="550458263" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8928" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8928/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8928">desktop#8928</a></li>
<li>Don't suggest creating a pull request if the current branch has an open pull request targeting an upstream repo - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="514062955" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8549" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8549/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8549">desktop#8549</a></li>
<li>Remove false branch protection warning when switching branches - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="532384394" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8743" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8743/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8743">desktop#8743</a></li>
<li>Show branch protection warning after checking out protected branches outside Desktop - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="537237813" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8790" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8790/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8790">desktop#8790</a></li>
<li>Only show branch protection warning when changed files are present - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="537592157" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8795" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8795/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8795">desktop#8795</a></li>
<li>Show an error when editing a Git configuration file fails due to existing lock file - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="553656257" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8956" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/8956/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/8956">desktop#8956</a></li>
<li>Update design and layout for GitHub Desktop preferences - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="535337518" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8774" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8774/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8774">desktop#8774</a></li>
</ul>
<p>For more information check out the <a href="https://desktop.github.com/release-notes/">release notes</a> on <a href="https://desktop.github.com/release-notes/">desktop.github.com</a>.</p>

    <h2>New Features</h2>
<ul>
<li>Syntax highlighting support for 20 more programming languages - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="429337819" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7217" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7217/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7217">desktop#7217</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/KennethSweezy/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/KennethSweezy">@KennethSweezy</a>!</li>
</ul>
<h2>Fixes</h2>
<ul>
<li>File checkboxes and line selection in diffs are not disabled when committing -  <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="289615528" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/3814" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/3814/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/3814">desktop#3814</a>  <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="371477746" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/5934" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/5934/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/5934">desktop#5934</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/HashimotoYT/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/HashimotoYT">@HashimotoYT</a>!</li>
<li>Small images are scaled down too much in two-up image rendering -  <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="443351017" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7520" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7520/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7520">desktop#7520</a></li>
<li>Manual conflict resolution for binary files always chooses same version -  <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="475567255" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8059" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8059/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8059">desktop#8059</a></li>
<li>Branch pruner errors on "orphaned" branches - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="470005279" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7983" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7983/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7983">desktop#7983</a></li>
<li>Prevent CodeMirror search plugin from stealing registered global keyboard shortcuts - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="476938155" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8068" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/8068/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/8068">desktop#8068</a></li>
<li>Error message could appear outside the boundary of its container - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="470613352" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7988" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7988/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7988">desktop#7988</a></li>
<li>Improved error handling when trying to rebase a ref that doesn't exist - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="461502662" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7881" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7881/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7881">desktop#7881</a></li>
<li>Expand hover area on repository list items - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="463903192" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7910" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7910/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7910">desktop#7910</a>. Thanks <a class="user-mention" data-hovercard-type="user" data-hovercard-url="/users/say25/hovercard" data-octo-click="hovercard-link-click" data-octo-dimensions="link_type:self" href="https://github.com/say25">@say25</a>!</li>
<li>Always fast forward recent branches after fetch - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="454549512" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7761" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7761/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7761">desktop#7761</a></li>

<ul>
<li>You can now choose to bring your changes with you to a new branch or stash them on the current branch when switching branches - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="377642765" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/6107" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/6107/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/6107">desktop#6107</a></li>
<li>Rebase your current branch onto another branch using a guided flow - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="372100070" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/5953" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/5953/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/5953">desktop#5953</a></li>
<li>Repositories grouped by owner, and recent repositories listed at top - <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="413521837" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/6923" data-hovercard-type="pull_request" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/pull/6923/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/pull/6923">desktop#6923</a> <a class="issue-link js-issue-link" data-error-text="Failed to load title" data-id="423766149" data-permission-text="Title is private" data-url="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7132" data-hovercard-type="issue" data-hovercard-url="/desktop/desktop/issues/7132/hovercard" href="https://github.com/desktop/desktop/issues/7132">desktop#7132</a></li>
